## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
```

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Domain Lineage: Kubernetes Watch Event Delivery Path

## Your Task

Trace how a Kubernetes watch event is generated and delivered from etcd to a client application. Find: 1. In `etcd-io/etcd`: the Go file that defines the `watchStream` or `serverWatchStream` that sends events from the etcd MVCC store. 2. In `kubernetes/kubernetes`: the Go files under `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/` that implement the watch cache and event distribution (look for `Cacher` and `watchCache`). 3. In the kubernetes client-go ecosystem: the Go file that defines the `Reflector` that receives watch events on the client side. Report the repo, file path, and struct/type name for each hop.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the domain domain.

## Available Resources

No local repositories are pre-checked out.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
*(none — all repos available locally)*

Done! I've created `/workspace/answer.json` with a comprehensive trace of the Kubernetes watch event delivery path. The answer includes:

**Key Components Found:**

1. **etcd-io/etcd** (`github.com/sg-evals/etcd-io-etcd`):
   - `watchStream` (server/mvcc/watcher.go) - MVCC layer that creates watch events
   - `serverWatchStream` (server/etcdserver/api/v3rpc/watch.go) - gRPC server handling watch requests

2. **Kubernetes API Server** (`github.com/sg-evals/kubernetes-kubernetes`):
   - `Cacher` (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/storage/cacher/cacher.go) - caches WATCH/LIST requests with event dispatching
   - `watchCache` (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/storage/cacher/watch_cache.go) - sliding window of recent changes
   - `WatchServer` (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/handlers/watch.go) - serves watch events over HTTP

3. **client-go** (`github.com/sg-evals/kubernetes-client-go`):
   - `Reflector` (tools/cache/reflector.go) - client-side watcher that receives events

The complete event flow goes: **etcd MVCC watchStream → etcd serverWatchStream (gRPC) → Kubernetes Cacher → watchCache → WatchServer (HTTP) → client Reflector**
